<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Prologue">Prologue</span></h4>
<div class="we"><div id="IMSLP347592" class="we_file_first we_fileblock_10">
<div class="we_file_download plainlinks">
<p><b><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://imslp.org/wiki/Special:ImagefromIndex/347592"><span title="Download this file"><span class="we_file_dlarrwrap"><span class="we_file_dlarrow">&#160;</span></span>Complete parts</span></a></b><br />

	<span class='current-rating' id='current-rating-347592' style='width:0%;'>0.0/10</span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Carnaval de Venise
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Opéra-ballet en 1 prologue et 3 actes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Campra,_Andr%C3%A9" title="Category:Campra, André">Campra, André</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IAC 6
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>Prologue and 3 acts (Act III with 2 divertissements)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1669-01-20 – Paris, Académie Royale de Musique
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1699 - Paris: C. Ballard
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Regnard,_Jean-Fran%C3%A7ois" title="Category:Regnard, Jean-François">Jean-François Regnard</a> (1655-1709)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>French
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>Voices, chorus and orchestra <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd><i>Roles</i> 
<dl><dd>l'Ordonnateur (Fa 4)<br />Minerve (Ut 1)<br />un des Arts (Ut 3)<br />Léonore (Ut 1)<br />Isabelle (Sol 2)<br />Lingras (Fa 4)<br />Léandre (Fa 4)<br />une Bohémienne (Sol 2)<br />l'Esclavon (Ut 3)<br />une Arménienne (Sol 2)<br />un Arménien (Ut 3)<br />Rodolphe (Fa 4)<br />la Fortune (Ut 1)<br />un Masque (Ut 3)<br />le Chef des Castellans (Ut 4)<br />une Gondolière (Ut 1) 
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Choeur</i> (Ut 1, Ut 3, Ut 4, Fa 4)
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i> 
<dl><dd>Sol 1, Ut 1, Ut 2, Ut 3, Fa 4<br />[including 2 flutes, 2 oboes, bassoons + strings] </span>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fr:Le_Carnaval_de_Venise_(Campra)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:fr:Le Carnaval de Venise (Campra)">Wikipedia article (French)</a><br /><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_carnaval_de_Venise" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Le carnaval de Venise">Wikipedia article (stub)</a>
</td></tr></table>
</div>
